						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
						has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
					}
					check_for_warlord_full = no
					check_for_warlord_7_left = no
					check_for_warlord_6_left = no
					check_for_warlord_5_left = no
					check_for_warlord_4_left = no
					check_for_warlord_3_left = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
								has_war = yes
							}
							has_country_flag = kmt_wont_remove_warlord_army
						}
					}
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
				}
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
				add_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
			}

			if = { #lower warlord clique penalty 2 left
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
						AND = {
							has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
							has_war = yes
						}
					}
					OR = {
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
						has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
					}
					check_for_warlord_full = no
					check_for_warlord_7_left = no
					check_for_warlord_6_left = no
					check_for_warlord_5_left = no
					check_for_warlord_4_left = no
					check_for_warlord_3_left = no
					check_for_warlord_2_left = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
								has_war = yes
							}
							has_country_flag = kmt_wont_remove_warlord_army
						}
					}
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
				}
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
				add_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
			}

			if = { #lower warlord clique penalty 1 left
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
						AND = {
							has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
							has_war = yes
						}
					}
					OR = {
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
						has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
					}
					check_for_warlord_full = no
					check_for_warlord_7_left = no
					check_for_warlord_6_left = no
					check_for_warlord_5_left = no
					check_for_warlord_4_left = no
					check_for_warlord_3_left = no
					check_for_warlord_2_left = no
					check_for_warlord_1_left = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
								has_war = yes
							}
							has_country_flag = kmt_wont_remove_warlord_army
						}
					}
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
				}
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
				add_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
			}

			if = { #remove warlord clique
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
					}
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_for_warlord_full = no
							check_for_warlord_7_left = no
							check_for_warlord_6_left = no
							check_for_warlord_5_left = no
							check_for_warlord_4_left = no
							check_for_warlord_3_left = no
							check_for_warlord_2_left = no
							check_for_warlord_1_left = no
							check_for_warlord_none = yes
						}
						AND = {
							has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
							has_war = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
								has_war = yes
							}
							has_country_flag = kmt_wont_remove_warlord_army
						}
					}
					remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
				}
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
			}

			if = { #wartime warlord clique
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = KMT_incorporate_warlord_forces
					}
					has_war = yes
					OR = {
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
						has_idea = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
					}
					OR = {
						GXC = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
						YUN = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
						XSM = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
						SHX = { is_in_faction_with = CHI }
						GXC = { exists = no }
						YUN = { exists = no }
						XSM = { exists = no }
						SHX = { exists = no }
						GXC = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
						YUN = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
						XSM = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
						SHX = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_pre_war
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_4
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_3
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_2
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_1
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_5
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_6
				remove_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_7
				add_ideas = KMT_warlord_cliques_war
			}
		}
	}

	on_peaceconference_ended = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = PAL
					FROM = { tag = ISR }
					controls_state = 454
				}
				country_event = palestine.61
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = ISR
					FROM = { tag = PAL }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = mandate_palestine.208
					days = 1 
					random_hours = 12
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_civil_war_end = { 
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					TAG = EGY
					PAL = {
						has_country_flag = PAL_palestinian_aided_uprising
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = palestine.45
					days = 1
					random_hours = 12
				}
			}
		}
	}
	on_monthly_MPL = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_power_balance = {
						id = MPL_power_balance
					}
				}
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = MPL_city_random
					min = 1
					max = 7
					integer = yes
				}
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = MPL_jew_militia
					min = 1
					max = 3
					integer = yes
				}
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = MPL_arab_militia
					min = 1
					max = 5
					integer = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = MPL_no_raid_chance
						}
						#DO NOTHING
					}
					1 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = MPL_raid_chance
						}
						#TRIGGER EVENT
						random_list = {
							30 = {
								country_event = { #Irgun wins clash
									id = mandate_palestine.301
									days = 1
									random_days = 25
									random_hours = 24
								}
							}
							30 = {
								country_event = { #Al Muqaddass wins clash
									id = mandate_palestine.302
									days = 1
									random_days = 25
									random_hours = 24
								}
							}
							15 = {
								country_event = { #Irgun attacks garrison
									id = mandate_palestine.303
									days = 1
									random_days = 25
									random_hours = 24
								}
							}
							15 = {
								country_event = { #Al Muqaddass attacks garrison
									id = mandate_palestine.304
									days = 1
									random_days = 25
									random_hours = 24
								}
							}
							5 = {
								country_event = { #Irgun seizes arms supply
									id = mandate_palestine.305
									days = 1
									random_days = 25
									random_hours = 24
								}
							}
							5 = {
								country_event = { #Al Muqaddass seizes arms supply
									id = mandate_palestine.306
									days = 1
									random_days = 25
									random_hours = 24
									}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
		}
	}
	
	on_monthly_DEN = {
		effect = {
			#
			# (E-L)/4 ~ diff/month
			# (50-75)/4 = -6.25 ~ -6
			# (50-20)/4 = 7.5 ~ 8
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = DEN
					den_stratas_enabled = yes
				}
				den_calculate_eqilibirum_monthly = yes
			}
		}
	}
